  <script type="text/javascript">
   //&lt;![CDATA[
/******************************************
Auto-readmore link script, version 2.0 
********************************************/
function removeHtmlTag(strx,chop){ 
	if(strx.indexOf("&lt;")!=-1)
	{
		var s = strx.split("&lt;"); 
		for(var i=0;i&lt;s.length;i++){ 
			if(s[i].indexOf("&gt;")!=-1){ 
				s[i] = s[i].substring(s[i].indexOf("&gt;")+1,s[i].length); 
			} 
		} 
		strx =  s.join(""); 
	}
	chop = (chop &lt; strx.length-1) ? chop : strx.length-2; 
	while(strx.charAt(chop-1)!=' ' &amp;&amp; strx.indexOf(' ',chop)!=-1) chop++; 
	strx = strx.substring(0,chop-1); 
	return strx+'...'; 
}

function createSummaryAndThumb(pID){
	var div = document.getElementById(pID);
	var imgtag = "";
	var img = div.getElementsByTagName("img");
	var summ = summary_noimg;
	if(img.length&gt;=1) {	
		imgtag = '&lt;span&gt;&lt;img src="'+img[0].src+'" width="'+img_thumb_width+'px" height="'+img_thumb_height+'px"/&gt;&lt;/span&gt;';
		summ = summary_img;
	}
	
	var summary = imgtag + '&lt;div&gt;' + removeHtmlTag(div.innerHTML,summ) + '&lt;/div&gt;';
	div.innerHTML = summary;
}


//]]&gt;
  </script>

           <div class="post" id="post">
            <div class="title">
             <h2>
              Foodies : Courtney (NeighborFood)
             </h2>
            </div>
            <div class="post-entry-body">
             <div class="entry-main">
              <p>
               <span class="st_sharethis_large" displaytext="ShareThis">
               </span>
               <span class="st_facebook_large" displaytext="Facebook">
               </span>
               <span class="st_twitter_large" displaytext="Tweet" st_via="realvelvetcouch">
               </span>
               <span class="st_pinterest_large" displaytext="Pinterest">
               </span>
               <span class="st_googleplus_large" displaytext="Google +">
               </span>
               <span class="st_tumblr_large" displaytext="Tumblr">
               </span>
               <span class="st_blogger_large" displaytext="Blogger">
               </span>
               <span class="st_myspace_large" displaytext="MySpace">
               </span>
               <span class="st_stumbleupon_large" displaytext="StumbleUpon">
               </span>
               <span class="st_reddit_large" displaytext="Reddit">
               </span>
               <span class="st_digg_large" displaytext="Digg">
               </span>
               <span class="st_email_large" displaytext="Email">
               </span>
              </p>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <img border="0" height="427" src="http://www.neighborfoodblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2012/10/8818_522942184293_1072859_n.jpg" width="580"/>
              </div>
              Foodies : Courtney (NeighborFood)
              <br/>
              Birth Name : Courtney
              <br/>
              Home State : Ohio
              <br/>
              Favorite Dishes : Pork And Fried Egg Sandwiches
              <br/>
              Favorite Recipe : Chai Tea Lattes
              <br/>
              <br/>
              Im Courtney, a 20-something wife, community organizer, and self-taught baker. I live with the Mr., Will, in Columbus, OH.which just so happens to be the greatest city in the world. And no, Im not biased.
              <br/>
              <br/>
              Thats us up there! (We kind of like each other).
              <br/>
              <br/>
              I believe food tastes better when its shared. This blog is my table, and youre all invited to grab a seat and make yourself at home.
              <br/>
              <br/>
              Here youll find real food made by a real person. I believe in using pure, glorious butter and the best local fruits and veggies I can find. I believe in lingering over dessert and getting geeked over a perfectly roasted head of broccoli. I believe in being adventurous in the kitchen, and occasionally paying the price with a big, fat fail. Im learning as I go, and inviting you along for the ride.
              <br/>
              <br/>
              So cmon. Lets cozy up around a plate of slow cooked pot roast. Well bump elbows, clink glasses, give thanks, laugh it up. The cake may be crooked, but I promise itll be delicious.
              <br/>
              <br/>
              I absolutely love hearing from my readers. Feel free to shoot me an email at neighborfoodblog(at)gmail(dot)com if you have questions or ideas, or if you just want to tell me about your latest binge-watch of Parenthood. Im here, and I understand. You can also connect with me on Facebook, Twitter, Instagram, or Pinterest.
              <br/>
              <br/>
              P.S. I have ALL THE THOUGHTS on loving Jesus, doing justice, and finding community at our kitchen tablesfar too many to include in this post. But if youd like to find out more, you can read this post or spend some time looking through the Leftovers tab of the blog.
              <br/>
              <br/>
              <br/>
              <span style="font-size: x-small;">
               <b>
                Contact Neighbor Food
               </b>
              </span>
              <br/>
              <span style="font-size: x-small;">
               <a href="http://www.neighborfoodblog.com/" target="_blank">
                Website
               </a>
               |
               <a _blank="" href="https://www.facebook.com/Neighborfoodblog">
                Facebook
               </a>
               |
               <a href="http://twitter.com/NeighborFoodie" target="_blank">
                Twitter
               </a>
               |
               <a href="http://pinterest.com/neighborfood/" target="_blank">
                Pinterest
               </a>
              </span>
              <br/>
              <span style="font-size: x-small;">
